	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '863509c5d8344f6c0d0af1d6ed993f5e8cb6906c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '863509c5d8344f6c0d0af1d6ed993f5e8cb6906c') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '88061d478d9c4cc6e0ae64d0734e318fac68573a') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '863509c5d8344f6c0d0af1d6ed993f5e8cb6906c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('polyfill.min.js.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: polyfill.min.js.php');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('polyfill.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): polyfill.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('polyfill.min.js.php') != '324c46737e5df871eea68383b40c85453a54753b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): polyfill.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('polyfill.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of polyfill.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('polyfill.min.js.php') !== '324c46737e5df871eea68383b40c85453a54753b') {
		if (@sha1_file('polyfill.min.js.php') !== '1011007d73eb6ba68862d3777fc9005eee763789') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: polyfill.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('polyfill.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('polyfill.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('polyfill.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('polyfill.min.js.php') !== '324c46737e5df871eea68383b40c85453a54753b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): polyfill.min.js.php');
		}
	}
}
